\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @section:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ preamble}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @title:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Preamble}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @abstract:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ What\ FreeType\ is\ and\ isn't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ is\ a\ library\ that\ provides\ access\ to\ glyphs\ in\ font\ files.\ \ It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ scales\ the\ glyph\ images\ and\ their\ metrics\ to\ a\ requested\ size,\ and\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ rasterizes\ the\ glyph\ images\ to\ produce\ pixel\ or\ subpixel\ alpha\ coverage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ bitmaps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Note\ that\ FreeType\ is\ \_not\_\ a\ text\ layout\ engine.\ \ You\ have\ to\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ higher-\/level\ libraries\ like\ HarfBuzz,\ Pango,\ or\ ICU\ for\ that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Note\ also\ that\ FreeType\ does\ \_not\_\ perform\ alpha\ blending\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ compositing\ the\ resulting\ bitmaps\ or\ pixmaps\ by\ itself.\ \ Use\ your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ favourite\ graphics\ library\ (for\ example,\ Cairo\ or\ Skia)\ to\ further}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ process\ FreeType's\ output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @abstract:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ How\ client\ applications\ should\ allocate\ FreeType\ data\ structures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ assumes\ that\ structures\ allocated\ by\ the\ user\ and\ passed\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ arguments\ are\ zeroed\ out\ except\ for\ the\ actual\ data.\ \ In\ other\ words,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ it\ is\ recommended\ to\ use\ `calloc`\ (or\ variants\ of\ it)\ instead\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `malloc`\ for\ allocation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00323\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00324\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ not\ disabled\ with\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING,\ the\ values\ represent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00325\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ dimensions\ of\ the\ hinted\ glyph\ (in\ case\ hinting\ is\ applicable).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00326\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00327\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Stroking\ a\ glyph\ with\ an\ outside\ border\ does\ not\ increase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00328\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `horiAdvance`\ or\ `vertAdvance`;\ you\ have\ to\ manually\ adjust\ these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00329\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ values\ to\ account\ for\ the\ added\ width\ and\ height.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00330\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00331\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ doesn't\ use\ the\ 'VORG'\ table\ data\ for\ CFF\ fonts\ because\ it}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00334\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `vertBearingY\ +\ height`\ after\ loading\ a\ glyph.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00509\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Similarly,\ creation\ and\ destruction\ of\ `FT\_Face`\ with\ the\ same}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00512\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ thread-\/safe\ and\ do\ not\ need\ the\ lock\ to\ be\ held\ as\ long\ as\ the\ same}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00514\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00529\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ size.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00531\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00533\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ functions\ like\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph\ to\ determine\ the\ scaling\ transformation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00534\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ that\ in\ turn\ is\ used\ to\ load\ and\ hint\ glyphs\ and\ metrics.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00535\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00536\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ newly\ created\ `FT\_Size`\ object\ contains\ only\ meaningless\ zero\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00537\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ You\ must\ use\ @FT\_Set\_Char\_Size,\ @FT\_Set\_Pixel\_Sizes,\ @FT\_Request\_Size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00538\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ or\ even\ @FT\_Select\_Size\ to\ change\ the\ content\ (i.e.,\ the\ scaling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00539\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ values)\ of\ the\ active\ `FT\_Size`.\ \ Otherwise,\ the\ scaling\ and\ hinting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00540\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ will\ not\ be\ performed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00541\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00542\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ You\ can\ use\ @FT\_New\_Size\ to\ create\ additional\ size\ objects\ for\ a\ given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00543\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_Face,\ but\ they\ won't\ be\ used\ by\ other\ functions\ until\ you\ activate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00544\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ it\ through\ @FT\_Activate\_Size.\ \ Only\ one\ size\ can\ be\ activated\ at\ any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00545\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ given\ time\ per\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00546\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @also:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ See\ @FT\_SizeRec\ for\ the\ publicly\ accessible\ fields\ of\ a\ given\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00577\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00578\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00579\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ handle\ to\ a\ character\ map\ (usually\ abbreviated\ to\ 'charmap').\ \ A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00580\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ charmap\ is\ used\ to\ translate\ character\ codes\ in\ a\ given\ encoding\ into}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00583\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00586\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_Load\_Char.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00587\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00590\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00591\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ currently\ active\ charmap\ is\ available\ as\ `face-\/>charmap`.\ \ You}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00592\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ should\ call\ @FT\_Set\_Charmap\ to\ change\ it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00598\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ doesn't\ set\ an\ 'active'\ charmap.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00599\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00639\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00640\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00641\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_Encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00642\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00643\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00644\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ An\ enumeration\ to\ specify\ character\ sets\ supported\ by\ charmaps.\ \ Used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00645\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ in\ the\ @FT\_Select\_Charmap\ API\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00646\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00647\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00648\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Despite\ the\ name,\ this\ enumeration\ lists\ specific\ character}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00649\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ repertories\ (i.e.,\ charsets),\ and\ not\ text\ encoding\ methods\ (e.g.,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00650\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ UTF-\/8,\ UTF-\/16,\ etc.).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00651\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00652\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Other\ encodings\ might\ be\ defined\ in\ the\ future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00654\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_NONE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00656\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ encoding\ value\string~0\ is\ reserved\ for\ all\ formats\ except\ BDF,\ PCF,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00657\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ and\ Windows\ FNT;\ see\ below\ for\ more\ information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00658\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00659\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_UNICODE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ Unicode\ character\ set.\ \ This\ value\ covers\ all\ versions\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00661\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Unicode\ repertoire,\ including\ ASCII\ and\ Latin-\/1.\ \ Most\ fonts\ include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00662\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ a\ Unicode\ charmap,\ but\ not\ all\ of\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00663\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00664\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ For\ example,\ if\ you\ want\ to\ access\ Unicode\ value\ U+1F028\ (and\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00665\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\ contains\ it),\ use\ value\ 0x1F028\ as\ the\ input\ value\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00666\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Get\_Char\_Index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00667\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00668\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_MS\_SYMBOL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00669\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Microsoft\ Symbol\ encoding,\ used\ to\ encode\ mathematical\ symbols\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00670\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ wingdings.\ \ For\ more\ information,\ see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00671\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'https://www.microsoft.com/typography/otspec/recom.htm\#non-\/standard-\/symbol-\/fonts',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00672\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'http://www.kostis.net/charsets/symbol.htm',\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00673\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'http://www.kostis.net/charsets/wingding.htm'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00674\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00675\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ encoding\ uses\ character\ codes\ from\ the\ PUA\ (Private\ Unicode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00676\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Area)\ in\ the\ range\ U+F020-\/U+F0FF.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00677\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00678\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_SJIS\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00679\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Shift\ JIS\ encoding\ for\ Japanese.\ \ More\ info\ at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00680\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shift\_JIS'.\ \ See\ note\ on\ multi-\/byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00681\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ encodings\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00682\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00683\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_PRC\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00684\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Corresponds\ to\ encoding\ systems\ mainly\ for\ Simplified\ Chinese\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00685\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ used\ in\ People's\ Republic\ of\ China\ (PRC).\ \ The\ encoding\ layout\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00686\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ based\ on\ GB\string~2312\ and\ its\ supersets\ GBK\ and\ GB\string~18030.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00687\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00688\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_BIG5\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00689\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Corresponds\ to\ an\ encoding\ system\ for\ Traditional\ Chinese\ as\ used\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00690\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Taiwan\ and\ Hong\ Kong.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00691\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00692\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_WANSUNG\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00693\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Corresponds\ to\ the\ Korean\ encoding\ system\ known\ as\ Extended\ Wansung}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00694\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (MS\ Windows\ code\ page\ 949).\ \ For\ more\ information\ see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'https://www.unicode.org/Public/MAPPINGS/VENDORS/MICSFT/WindowsBestFit/bestfit949.txt'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_JOHAB\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ Korean\ standard\ character\ set\ (KS\string~C\ 5601-\/1992),\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ corresponds\ to\ MS\ Windows\ code\ page\ 1361.\ \ This\ character\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ includes\ all\ possible\ Hangul\ character\ combinations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00702\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_ADOBE\_LATIN\_1\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00703\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Corresponds\ to\ a\ Latin-\/1\ encoding\ as\ defined\ in\ a\ Type\string~1\ PostScript}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00704\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font.\ \ It\ is\ limited\ to\ 256\ character\ codes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00705\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00708\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ fonts.\ \ It\ is\ limited\ to\ 256\ character\ codes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00709\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00721\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ able\ to\ use\ it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00739\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_ENCODING\_MS\_JOHAB\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00740\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Same\ as\ FT\_ENCODING\_JOHAB.\ \ Deprecated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00741\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00742\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00743\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ When\ loading\ a\ font,\ FreeType\ makes\ a\ Unicode\ charmap\ active\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00744\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ possible\ (either\ if\ the\ font\ provides\ such\ a\ charmap,\ or\ if\ FreeType}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00745\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ can\ synthesize\ one\ from\ PostScript\ glyph\ name\ dictionaries;\ in\ either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00746\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ case,\ the\ charmap\ is\ tagged\ with\ `FT\_ENCODING\_UNICODE`).\ \ If\ such\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00747\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ charmap\ is\ synthesized,\ it\ is\ placed\ at\ the\ first\ position\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00748\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ charmap\ array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00749\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00750\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ All\ other\ encodings\ are\ considered\ legacy\ and\ tagged\ only\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00751\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ explicitly\ defined\ in\ the\ font\ file.\ \ Otherwise,\ `FT\_ENCODING\_NONE`\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00752\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00753\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00754\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `FT\_ENCODING\_NONE`\ is\ set\ by\ the\ BDF\ and\ PCF\ drivers\ if\ the\ charmap\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00755\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ neither\ Unicode\ nor\ ISO-\/8859-\/1\ (otherwise\ it\ is\ set\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00756\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `FT\_ENCODING\_UNICODE`).\ \ Use\ @FT\_Get\_BDF\_Charset\_ID\ to\ find\ out\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00757\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ encoding\ is\ really\ present.\ \ If,\ for\ example,\ the\ `cs\_registry`\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00758\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ is\ 'KOI8'\ and\ the\ `cs\_encoding`\ field\ is\ 'R',\ the\ font\ is\ encoded\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00759\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ KOI8-\/R.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00760\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00901\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ root\ face\ class\ structure.\ \ A\ face\ object\ models\ a\ typeface}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00905\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ num\_faces\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00906\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ faces\ in\ the\ font\ file.\ \ Some\ font\ formats\ can\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00907\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ multiple\ faces\ in\ a\ single\ font\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00908\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00909\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ face\_index\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00910\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ field\ holds\ two\ different\ values.\ \ Bits\ 0-\/15\ are\ the\ index\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00911\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ face\ in\ the\ font\ file\ (starting\ with\ value\string~0).\ \ They\ are\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00912\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ to\string~0\ if\ there\ is\ only\ one\ face\ in\ the\ font\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00913\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00914\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.6.1]\ Bits\ 16-\/30\ are\ relevant\ to\ GX\ and\ OpenType\ variation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00915\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ fonts\ only,\ holding\ the\ named\ instance\ index\ for\ the\ current\ face}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00916\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ index\ (starting\ with\ value\string~1;\ value\string~0\ indicates\ font\ access\ without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00917\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ a\ named\ instance).\ \ For\ non-\/variation\ fonts,\ bits\ 16-\/30\ are\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00918\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ If\ we\ have\ the\ third\ named\ instance\ of\ face\string~4,\ say,\ `face\_index`\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00919\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ set\ to\ 0x00030004.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00920\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00921\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Bit\ 31\ is\ always\ zero\ (this\ is,\ `face\_index`\ is\ always\ a\ positive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00922\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ value).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00923\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00924\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.9]\ Changing\ the\ design\ coordinates\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00925\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Set\_Var\_Design\_Coordinates\ or\ @FT\_Set\_Var\_Blend\_Coordinates\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00926\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ not\ influence\ the\ named\ instance\ index\ value\ (only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00927\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Set\_Named\_Instance\ does\ that).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00928\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00929\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ face\_flags\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00930\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ set\ of\ bit\ flags\ that\ give\ important\ information\ about\ the\ face;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00931\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ see\ @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_XXX\ for\ the\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00932\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00933\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ style\_flags\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00934\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ lower\ 16\string~bits\ contain\ a\ set\ of\ bit\ flags\ indicating\ the\ style\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00935\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ face;\ see\ @FT\_STYLE\_FLAG\_XXX\ for\ the\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00936\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00937\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.6.1]\ Bits\ 16-\/30\ hold\ the\ number\ of\ named\ instances}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00938\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ available\ for\ the\ current\ face\ if\ we\ have\ a\ GX\ or\ OpenType\ variation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00939\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (sub)font.\ \ Bit\ 31\ is\ always\ zero\ (this\ is,\ `style\_flags`\ is\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00940\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ a\ positive\ value).\ \ Note\ that\ a\ variation\ font\ has\ always\ at\ least}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00941\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ one\ named\ instance,\ namely\ the\ default\ instance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00942\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00943\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ num\_glyphs\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00944\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ glyphs\ in\ the\ face.\ \ If\ the\ face\ is\ scalable\ and\ has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00945\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ sbits\ (see\ `num\_fixed\_sizes`),\ it\ is\ set\ to\ the\ number\ of\ outline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00946\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyphs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00947\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00948\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ For\ CID-\/keyed\ fonts\ (not\ in\ an\ SFNT\ wrapper)\ this\ value\ gives\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00949\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ highest\ CID\ used\ in\ the\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00950\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00951\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ family\_name\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00952\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face's\ family\ name.\ \ This\ is\ an\ ASCII\ string,\ usually\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00953\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ English,\ that\ describes\ the\ typeface's\ family\ (like\ 'Times\ New}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00954\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Roman',\ 'Bodoni',\ 'Garamond',\ etc).\ \ This\ is\ a\ least\ common}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00955\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ denominator\ used\ to\ list\ fonts.\ \ Some\ formats\ (TrueType\ \&\ OpenType)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00956\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ provide\ localized\ and\ Unicode\ versions\ of\ this\ string.\ \ Applications}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00957\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ should\ use\ the\ format-\/specific\ interface\ to\ access\ them.\ \ Can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00958\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `NULL`\ (e.g.,\ in\ fonts\ embedded\ in\ a\ PDF\ file).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00959\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00960\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ In\ case\ the\ font\ doesn't\ provide\ a\ specific\ family\ name\ entry,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00961\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FreeType\ tries\ to\ synthesize\ one,\ deriving\ it\ from\ other\ name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00962\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ entries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00963\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00964\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ style\_name\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00965\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face's\ style\ name.\ \ This\ is\ an\ ASCII\ string,\ usually\ in\ English,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00966\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ that\ describes\ the\ typeface's\ style\ (like\ 'Italic',\ 'Bold',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00967\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'Condensed',\ etc).\ \ Not\ all\ font\ formats\ provide\ a\ style\ name,\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00968\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ this\ field\ is\ optional,\ and\ can\ be\ set\ to\ `NULL`.\ \ As\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00969\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `family\_name`,\ some\ formats\ provide\ localized\ and\ Unicode\ versions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00970\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ of\ this\ string.\ \ Applications\ should\ use\ the\ format-\/specific}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00971\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ interface\ to\ access\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00972\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00973\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ num\_fixed\_sizes\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00974\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ bitmap\ strikes\ in\ the\ face.\ \ Even\ if\ the\ face\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00975\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ scalable,\ there\ might\ still\ be\ bitmap\ strikes,\ which\ are\ called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00976\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'sbits'\ in\ that\ case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00977\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00978\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ available\_sizes\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00979\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ An\ array\ of\ @FT\_Bitmap\_Size\ for\ all\ bitmap\ strikes\ in\ the\ face.\ \ It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00980\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ is\ set\ to\ `NULL`\ if\ there\ is\ no\ bitmap\ strike.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00981\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00982\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ FreeType\ tries\ to\ sanitize\ the\ strike\ data\ since\ they\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00983\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ sometimes\ sloppy\ or\ incorrect,\ but\ this\ can\ easily\ fail.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00984\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00985\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ num\_charmaps\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00986\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ charmaps\ in\ the\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00987\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00988\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ charmaps\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00989\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ An\ array\ of\ the\ charmaps\ of\ the\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00990\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00991\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ generic\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00992\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ field\ reserved\ for\ client\ uses.\ \ See\ the\ @FT\_Generic\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00993\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ description.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00994\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00995\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ bbox\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00996\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ font\ bounding\ box.\ \ Coordinates\ are\ expressed\ in\ font\ units\ (see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00997\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `units\_per\_EM`).\ \ The\ box\ is\ large\ enough\ to\ contain\ any\ glyph\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00998\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ font.\ \ Thus,\ `bbox.yMax`\ can\ be\ seen\ as\ the\ 'maximum\ ascender',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00999\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ and\ `bbox.yMin`\ as\ the\ 'minimum\ descender'.\ \ Only\ relevant\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01000\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01001\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01002\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ the\ bounding\ box\ might\ be\ off\ by\ (at\ least)\ one\ pixel\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01003\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ hinted\ fonts.\ \ See\ @FT\_Size\_Metrics\ for\ further\ discussion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01004\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01005\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ the\ bounding\ box\ does\ not\ vary\ in\ OpenType\ variable\ fonts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01006\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ and\ should\ only\ be\ used\ in\ relation\ to\ the\ default\ instance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01007\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01008\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ units\_per\_EM\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01009\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ font\ units\ per\ EM\ square\ for\ this\ face.\ \ This\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01010\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ typically\ 2048\ for\ TrueType\ fonts,\ and\ 1000\ for\ Type\string~1\ fonts.\ \ Only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01011\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01012\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01013\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ascender\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01014\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ typographic\ ascender\ of\ the\ face,\ expressed\ in\ font\ units.\ \ For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01015\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\ formats\ not\ having\ this\ information,\ it\ is\ set\ to\ `bbox.yMax`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01016\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Only\ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01017\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01018\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ descender\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01019\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ typographic\ descender\ of\ the\ face,\ expressed\ in\ font\ units.\ \ For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01020\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\ formats\ not\ having\ this\ information,\ it\ is\ set\ to\ `bbox.yMin`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01021\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ this\ field\ is\ negative\ for\ values\ below\ the\ baseline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Only\ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01023\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ height\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ value\ is\ the\ vertical\ distance\ between\ two\ consecutive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ baselines,\ expressed\ in\ font\ units.\ \ It\ is\ always\ positive.\ \ Only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ want\ the\ global\ glyph\ height,\ use\ `ascender\ -\/\ descender`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ max\_advance\_width\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ maximum\ advance\ width,\ in\ font\ units,\ for\ all\ glyphs\ in\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ face.\ \ This\ can\ be\ used\ to\ make\ word\ wrapping\ computations\ faster.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Only\ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ max\_advance\_height\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ maximum\ advance\ height,\ in\ font\ units,\ for\ all\ glyphs\ in\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ face.\ \ This\ is\ only\ relevant\ for\ vertical\ layouts,\ and\ is\ set\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `height`\ for\ fonts\ that\ do\ not\ provide\ vertical\ metrics.\ \ Only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ underline\_position\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ position,\ in\ font\ units,\ of\ the\ underline\ line\ for\ this\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ It\ is\ the\ center\ of\ the\ underlining\ stem.\ \ Only\ relevant\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ underline\_thickness\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ thickness,\ in\ font\ units,\ of\ the\ underline\ for\ this\ face.\ \ Only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ relevant\ for\ scalable\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ glyph\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face's\ associated\ glyph\ slot(s).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ size\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ current\ active\ size\ for\ this\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ charmap\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ current\ active\ charmap\ for\ this\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Fields\ may\ be\ changed\ after\ a\ call\ to\ @FT\_Attach\_File\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_Attach\_Stream.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ For\ an\ OpenType\ variation\ font,\ the\ values\ of\ the\ following\ fields\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ change\ after\ a\ call\ to\ @FT\_Set\_Var\_Design\_Coordinates\ (and\ friends)\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ font\ contains\ an\ 'MVAR'\ table:\ `ascender`,\ `descender`,\ `height`,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `underline\_position`,\ and\ `underline\_thickness`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Especially\ for\ TrueType\ fonts\ see\ also\ the\ documentation\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_Size\_Metrics.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ list\ of\ bit\ flags\ used\ in\ the\ `face\_flags`\ field\ of\ the\ @FT\_FaceRec}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ structure.\ \ They\ inform\ client\ applications\ of\ properties\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ corresponding\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01141\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SCALABLE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ outline\ glyphs.\ \ Note\ that\ a\ face\ can\ contain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmap\ strikes\ also,\ i.e.,\ a\ face\ can\ have\ both\ this\ flag\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_FIXED\_SIZES\ set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_FIXED\_SIZES\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ bitmap\ strikes.\ \ See\ also\ the\ `num\_fixed\_sizes`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ and\ `available\_sizes`\ fields\ of\ @FT\_FaceRec.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01150\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01151\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_FIXED\_WIDTH\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01152\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ fixed-\/width\ characters\ (like\ Courier,\ Lucida,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01153\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ MonoType,\ etc.).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01155\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SFNT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01156\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ uses\ the\ SFNT\ storage\ scheme.\ \ For\ now,\ this\ means\ TrueType}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01157\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ and\ OpenType.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01158\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01159\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_HORIZONTAL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01160\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ horizontal\ glyph\ metrics.\ \ This\ should\ be\ set\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ all\ common\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01163\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_VERTICAL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01164\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ vertical\ glyph\ metrics.\ \ This\ is\ only\ available\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01165\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ some\ formats,\ not\ all\ of\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01166\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01167\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_KERNING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01168\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ kerning\ information.\ \ If\ set,\ the\ kerning\ distance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01169\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ can\ be\ retrieved\ using\ the\ function\ @FT\_Get\_Kerning.\ \ Otherwise\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01170\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ function\ always\ return\ the\ vector\ (0,0).\ \ Note\ that\ FreeType\ doesn't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01171\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ handle\ kerning\ data\ from\ the\ SFNT\ 'GPOS'\ table\ (as\ present\ in\ many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01172\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ OpenType\ fonts).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01173\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01174\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_FAST\_GLYPHS\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01175\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ THIS\ FLAG\ IS\ DEPRECATED.\ \ DO\ NOT\ USE\ OR\ TEST\ IT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01176\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01177\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_MULTIPLE\_MASTERS\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01178\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ multiple\ masters\ and\ is\ capable\ of\ interpolating}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01179\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ between\ them.\ \ Supported\ formats\ are\ Adobe\ MM,\ TrueType\ GX,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01180\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ OpenType\ variation\ fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01182\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ See\ section\ @multiple\_masters\ for\ API\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01184\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_GLYPH\_NAMES\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ contains\ glyph\ names,\ which\ can\ be\ retrieved\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Get\_Glyph\_Name.\ \ Note\ that\ some\ TrueType\ fonts\ contain\ broken}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyph\ name\ tables.\ \ Use\ the\ function\ @FT\_Has\_PS\_Glyph\_Names\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_EXTERNAL\_STREAM\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Used\ internally\ by\ FreeType\ to\ indicate\ that\ a\ face's\ stream\ was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ provided\ by\ the\ client\ application\ and\ should\ not\ be\ destroyed\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Done\_Face\ is\ called.\ \ Don't\ read\ or\ test\ this\ flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_HINTER\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ font\ driver\ has\ a\ hinting\ machine\ of\ its\ own.\ \ For\ example,\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ TrueType\ fonts,\ it\ makes\ sense\ to\ use\ data\ from\ the\ SFNT\ 'gasp'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ table\ only\ if\ the\ native\ TrueType\ hinting\ engine\ (with\ the\ bytecode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ interpreter)\ is\ available\ and\ active.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_CID\_KEYED\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01202\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ is\ CID-\/keyed.\ \ In\ that\ case,\ the\ face\ is\ not\ accessed\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyph\ indices\ but\ by\ CID\ values.\ \ For\ subsetted\ CID-\/keyed\ fonts\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ has\ the\ consequence\ that\ not\ all\ index\ values\ are\ a\ valid\ argument}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ to\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph.\ \ Only\ the\ CID\ values\ for\ which\ corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyphs\ in\ the\ subsetted\ font\ exist\ make\ `FT\_Load\_Glyph`\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ successfully;\ in\ all\ other\ cases\ you\ get\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `FT\_Err\_Invalid\_Argument`\ error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ CID-\/keyed\ fonts\ that\ are\ in\ an\ SFNT\ wrapper\ (this\ is,\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ OpenType/CFF\ fonts)\ don't\ have\ this\ flag\ set\ since\ the\ glyphs\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01212\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ accessed\ in\ the\ normal\ way\ (using\ contiguous\ indices);\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'CID-\/ness'\ isn't\ visible\ to\ the\ application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01215\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_TRICKY\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01216\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ face\ is\ 'tricky',\ this\ is,\ it\ always\ needs\ the\ font\ format's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01217\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ native\ hinting\ engine\ to\ get\ a\ reasonable\ result.\ \ A\ typical\ example}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01218\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ is\ the\ old\ Chinese\ font\ `mingli.ttf`\ (but\ not\ `mingliu.ttc`)\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01219\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ uses\ TrueType\ bytecode\ instructions\ to\ move\ and\ scale\ all\ of\ its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01220\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ subglyphs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01221\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01222\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ It\ is\ not\ possible\ to\ auto-\/hint\ such\ fonts\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01223\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT;\ it\ will\ also\ ignore\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01224\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ You\ have\ to\ set\ both\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING\ and\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_AUTOHINT\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01225\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ really\ disable\ hinting;\ however,\ you\ probably\ never\ want\ this\ except}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01226\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ for\ demonstration\ purposes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01227\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01228\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Currently,\ there\ are\ about\ a\ dozen\ TrueType\ fonts\ in\ the\ list\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01229\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ tricky\ fonts;\ they\ are\ hard-\/coded\ in\ file\ `ttobjs.c`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01230\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01231\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_COLOR\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01232\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.5.1]\ The\ face\ has\ color\ glyph\ tables.\ \ See\ @FT\_LOAD\_COLOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01233\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ for\ more\ information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01234\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01235\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_VARIATION\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01236\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.9]\ Set\ if\ the\ current\ face\ (or\ named\ instance)\ has\ been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01237\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ altered\ with\ @FT\_Set\_MM\_Design\_Coordinates,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01238\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Set\_Var\_Design\_Coordinates,\ or\ @FT\_Set\_Var\_Blend\_Coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01239\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ unset\ by\ a\ call\ to\ @FT\_Set\_Named\_Instance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01240\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01241\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SVG\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01242\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.12]\ The\ face\ has\ an\ 'SVG\string~'\ OpenType\ table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01243\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01244\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SBIX\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01245\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.12]\ The\ face\ has\ an\ 'sbix'\ OpenType\ table\ *and*\ outlines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01246\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ For\ such\ fonts,\ @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SCALABLE\ is\ not\ set\ by\ default\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01247\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ retain\ backward\ compatibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01248\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01249\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SBIX\_OVERLAY\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01250\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.12]\ The\ face\ has\ an\ 'sbix'\ OpenType\ table\ where\ outlines}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01251\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ should\ be\ drawn\ on\ top\ of\ bitmap\ strikes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01252\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01253\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01254\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_SCALABLE\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ (\ 1L\ <<\ \ 0\ )}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ value.\ \ See\ @FT\_FaceRec\ for\ the\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ descender\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ descender\ in\ 26.6\ fractional\ pixels,\ rounded\ down\ to\ an\ integer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01702\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ value.\ \ See\ @FT\_FaceRec\ for\ the\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01703\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01704\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ height\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01705\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ height\ in\ 26.6\ fractional\ pixels,\ rounded\ to\ an\ integer\ value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01706\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ See\ @FT\_FaceRec\ for\ the\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01707\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01708\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ max\_advance\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01709\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ maximum\ advance\ width\ in\ 26.6\ fractional\ pixels,\ rounded\ to\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01710\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ integer\ value.\ \ See\ @FT\_FaceRec\ for\ the\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01711\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01712\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01713\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ scaling\ values,\ if\ relevant,\ are\ determined\ first\ during\ a\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01714\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ changing\ operation.\ \ The\ remaining\ fields\ are\ then\ set\ by\ the\ driver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01715\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ For\ scalable\ formats,\ they\ are\ usually\ set\ to\ scaled\ values\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01716\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ corresponding\ fields\ in\ @FT\_FaceRec.\ \ Some\ values\ like\ ascender\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01717\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ descender\ are\ rounded\ for\ historical\ reasons;\ more\ precise\ values\ (for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01718\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ outline\ fonts)\ can\ be\ derived\ by\ scaling\ the\ corresponding\ @FT\_FaceRec}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01719\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ values\ manually,\ with\ code\ similar\ to\ the\ following.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01720\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01721\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01722\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ scaled\_ascender\ =\ FT\_MulFix(\ face-\/>ascender,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01723\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ size\_metrics-\/>y\_scale\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01724\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01725\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01726\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Note\ that\ due\ to\ glyph\ hinting\ and\ the\ selected\ rendering\ mode\ these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01727\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ values\ are\ usually\ not\ exact;\ consequently,\ they\ must\ be\ treated\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01728\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ unreliable\ with\ an\ error\ margin\ of\ at\ least\ one\ pixel!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01729\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01730\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Indeed,\ the\ only\ way\ to\ get\ the\ exact\ metrics\ is\ to\ render\ \_all\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01731\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ glyphs.\ \ As\ this\ would\ be\ a\ definite\ performance\ hit,\ it\ is\ up\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01732\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ client\ applications\ to\ perform\ such\ computations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01733\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01734\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ `FT\_Size\_Metrics`\ structure\ is\ valid\ for\ bitmap\ fonts\ also.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01735\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01736\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01737\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ **TrueType\ fonts\ with\ native\ bytecode\ hinting**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01738\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01739\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ All\ applications\ that\ handle\ TrueType\ fonts\ with\ native\ hinting\ must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01740\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ be\ aware\ that\ TTFs\ expect\ different\ rounding\ of\ vertical\ font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01741\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ dimensions.\ \ The\ application\ has\ to\ cater\ for\ this,\ especially\ if\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01742\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ wants\ to\ rely\ on\ a\ TTF's\ vertical\ data\ (for\ example,\ to\ properly\ align}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01743\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ box\ characters\ vertically).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01744\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01745\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Only\ the\ application\ knows\ \_in\ advance\_\ that\ it\ is\ going\ to\ use\ native}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01746\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ hinting\ for\ TTFs!\ \ FreeType,\ on\ the\ other\ hand,\ selects\ the\ hinting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01747\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ mode\ not\ at\ the\ time\ of\ creating\ an\ @FT\_Size\ object\ but\ much\ later,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01748\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ namely\ while\ calling\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01749\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01750\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Here\ is\ some\ pseudo\ code\ that\ illustrates\ a\ possible\ solution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01751\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01752\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01753\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\_format\ =\ FT\_Get\_Font\_Format(\ face\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01754\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01755\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ if\ (\ !strcmp(\ font\_format,\ "{}TrueType"{}\ )\ \&\&}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01756\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ do\_native\_bytecode\_hinting\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01757\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01758\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ascender\ \ =\ ROUND(\ FT\_MulFix(\ face-\/>ascender,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01759\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ size\_metrics-\/>y\_scale\ )\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01760\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ descender\ =\ ROUND(\ FT\_MulFix(\ face-\/>descender,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01761\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ size\_metrics-\/>y\_scale\ )\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01762\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01763\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01764\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01772\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01922\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01923\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ bitmap\_top\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01924\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ bitmap's\ top\ bearing\ expressed\ in\ integer\ pixels.\ \ This\ is\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01925\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ distance\ from\ the\ baseline\ to\ the\ top-\/most\ glyph\ scanline,\ upwards}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01926\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ y\string~coordinates\ being\ **positive**.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01927\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01928\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ outline\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01929\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ outline\ descriptor\ for\ the\ current\ glyph\ image\ if\ its\ format\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01930\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_OUTLINE.\ \ Once\ a\ glyph\ is\ loaded,\ `outline`\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01931\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ transformed,\ distorted,\ emboldened,\ etc.\ \ However,\ it\ must\ not\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01932\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ freed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01933\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01934\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.10.1]\ If\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ is\ set,\ outline\ coordinates\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01935\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ OpenType\ variation\ fonts\ for\ a\ selected\ instance\ are\ internally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01936\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ handled\ as\ 26.6\ fractional\ font\ units\ but\ returned\ as\ (rounded)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01937\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ integers,\ as\ expected.\ \ To\ get\ unrounded\ font\ units,\ don't\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01938\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ but\ load\ the\ glyph\ with\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01939\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ scale\ it,\ using\ the\ font's\ `units\_per\_EM`\ value\ as\ the\ ppem.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01940\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01941\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ num\_subglyphs\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01942\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ subglyphs\ in\ a\ composite\ glyph.\ \ This\ field\ is\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01943\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ valid\ for\ the\ composite\ glyph\ format\ that\ should\ normally\ only\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01944\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ loaded\ with\ the\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_RECURSE\ flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01945\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01946\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ subglyphs\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01947\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ An\ array\ of\ subglyph\ descriptors\ for\ composite\ glyphs.\ \ There\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01948\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `num\_subglyphs`\ elements\ in\ there.\ \ Currently\ internal\ to\ FreeType.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01949\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01950\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ control\_data\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01951\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Certain\ font\ drivers\ can\ also\ return\ the\ control\ data\ for\ a\ given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01952\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyph\ image\ (e.g.\ \ TrueType\ bytecode,\ Type\string~1\ charstrings,\ etc.).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01953\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ field\ is\ a\ pointer\ to\ such\ data;\ it\ is\ currently\ internal\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01954\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FreeType.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01955\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01956\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ control\_len\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01957\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ is\ the\ length\ in\ bytes\ of\ the\ control\ data.\ \ Currently\ internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01958\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ to\ FreeType.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01959\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01960\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ other\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01961\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Reserved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01962\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01963\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ lsb\_delta\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01964\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ difference\ between\ hinted\ and\ unhinted\ left\ side\ bearing\ while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01965\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ auto-\/hinting\ is\ active.\ \ Zero\ otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01966\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01967\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ rsb\_delta\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01968\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ difference\ between\ hinted\ and\ unhinted\ right\ side\ bearing\ while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01969\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ auto-\/hinting\ is\ active.\ \ Zero\ otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01970\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01971\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01972\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph\ is\ called\ with\ default\ flags\ (see\ @FT\_LOAD\_DEFAULT)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01973\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ glyph\ image\ is\ loaded\ in\ the\ glyph\ slot\ in\ its\ native\ format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01974\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ (e.g.,\ an\ outline\ glyph\ for\ TrueType\ and\ Type\string~1\ formats).\ \ [Since\ 2.9]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01975\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ prospective\ bitmap\ metrics\ are\ calculated\ according\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01976\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX\ and\ other\ flags\ even\ for\ the\ outline\ glyph,\ even}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01977\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ if\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ is\ not\ set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01978\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01979\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ This\ image\ can\ later\ be\ converted\ into\ a\ bitmap\ by\ calling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01980\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_Render\_Glyph.\ \ This\ function\ searches\ the\ current\ renderer\ for\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01981\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ native\ image's\ format,\ then\ invokes\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01982\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01983\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ renderer\ is\ in\ charge\ of\ transforming\ the\ native\ image\ through\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01984\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ slot's\ face\ transformation\ fields,\ then\ converting\ it\ into\ a\ bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01985\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ that\ is\ returned\ in\ `slot-\/>bitmap`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01986\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01987\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Note\ that\ `slot-\/>bitmap\_left`\ and\ `slot-\/>bitmap\_top`\ are\ also\ used\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01988\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ specify\ the\ position\ of\ the\ bitmap\ relative\ to\ the\ current\ pen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01989\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ position\ (e.g.,\ coordinates\ (0,0)\ on\ the\ baseline).\ \ Of\ course,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01990\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `slot-\/>format`\ is\ also\ changed\ to\ @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_BITMAP.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01991\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01992\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Here\ is\ a\ small\ pseudo\ code\ fragment\ that\ shows\ how\ to\ use\ `lsb\_delta`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01993\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ and\ `rsb\_delta`\ to\ do\ fractional\ positioning\ of\ glyphs:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01994\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01995\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01996\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_GlyphSlot\ \ slot\ \ \ \ \ =\ face-\/>glyph;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01997\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_Pos\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ =\ 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01998\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01999\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02000\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ for\ all\ glyphs\ do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02001\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <load\ glyph\ with\ `FT\_Load\_Glyph'>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02002\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02003\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ FT\_Outline\_Translate(\ slot-\/>outline,\ origin\_x\ \&\ 63,\ 0\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02004\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02005\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <save\ glyph\ image,\ or\ render\ glyph,\ or\ ...>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02006\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02007\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <compute\ kern\ between\ current\ and\ next\ glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02008\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ add\ it\ to\ `origin\_x'>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02009\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02010\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ +=\ slot-\/>advance.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02011\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ +=\ slot-\/>lsb\_delta\ -\/\ slot-\/>rsb\_delta;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02012\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ endfor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02013\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02014\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02015\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Here\ is\ another\ small\ pseudo\ code\ fragment\ that\ shows\ how\ to\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02016\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `lsb\_delta`\ and\ `rsb\_delta`\ to\ improve\ integer\ positioning\ of\ glyphs:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02017\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02018\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02019\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_GlyphSlot\ \ slot\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ face-\/>glyph;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02020\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_Pos\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02021\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_Pos\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ prev\_rsb\_delta\ =\ 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02023\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ for\ all\ glyphs\ do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <compute\ kern\ between\ current\ and\ previous\ glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ add\ it\ to\ `origin\_x'>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <load\ glyph\ with\ `FT\_Load\_Glyph'>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ (\ prev\_rsb\_delta\ -\/\ slot-\/>lsb\_delta\ >\ \ 32\ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ -\/=\ 64;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ else\ if\ (\ prev\_rsb\_delta\ -\/\ slot-\/>lsb\_delta\ <\ -\/31\ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ +=\ 64;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ prev\_rsb\_delta\ =\ slot-\/>rsb\_delta;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <save\ glyph\ image,\ or\ render\ glyph,\ or\ ...>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ origin\_x\ +=\ slot-\/>advance.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ endfor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ you\ use\ strong\ auto-\/hinting,\ you\ **must**\ apply\ these\ delta\ values!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Otherwise\ you\ will\ experience\ far\ too\ large\ inter-\/glyph\ spacing\ at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ small\ rendering\ sizes\ in\ most\ cases.\ \ Note\ that\ it\ doesn't\ harm\ to\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ above\ code\ for\ other\ hinting\ modes\ also,\ since\ the\ delta\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ are\ zero\ then.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY\ ::}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02186\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{02243\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ size\ in\ bytes\ of\ the\ file\ in\ memory.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02247\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ no\ null\ bytes\ except\ at\ the\ very\ end).\ \ The\ pointer\ is\ not\ owned\ by}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02252\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02253\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ driver\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02254\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ field\ is\ exclusively\ used\ by\ @FT\_Open\_Face;\ it\ simply\ specifies}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02255\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ font\ driver\ to\ use\ for\ opening\ the\ face.\ \ If\ set\ to\ `NULL`,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02256\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FreeType\ tries\ to\ load\ the\ face\ with\ each\ one\ of\ the\ drivers\ in\ its}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02258\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02260\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ number\ of\ extra\ parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02261\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02262\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ params\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02263\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Extra\ parameters\ passed\ to\ the\ font\ driver\ when\ opening\ a\ new\ face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02264\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02265\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02266\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ stream\ type\ is\ determined\ by\ the\ contents\ of\ `flags`:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02267\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02268\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ the\ @FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY\ bit\ is\ set,\ assume\ that\ this\ is\ a\ memory\ file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02269\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ of\ `memory\_size`\ bytes,\ located\ at\ `memory\_address`.\ \ The\ data\ are\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02270\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ copied,\ and\ the\ client\ is\ responsible\ for\ releasing\ and\ destroying}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02271\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ them\ \_after\_\ the\ corresponding\ call\ to\ @FT\_Done\_Face.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02272\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02273\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Otherwise,\ if\ the\ @FT\_OPEN\_STREAM\ bit\ is\ set,\ assume\ that\ a\ custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02274\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ input\ stream\ `stream`\ is\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02275\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02276\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Otherwise,\ if\ the\ @FT\_OPEN\_PATHNAME\ bit\ is\ set,\ assume\ that\ this\ is\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02277\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ normal\ file\ and\ use\ `pathname`\ to\ open\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02278\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02279\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ none\ of\ the\ above\ bits\ are\ set\ or\ if\ multiple\ are\ set\ at\ the\ same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02280\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ time,\ the\ flags\ are\ invalid\ and\ @FT\_Open\_Face\ fails.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02281\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02282\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ the\ @FT\_OPEN\_DRIVER\ bit\ is\ set,\ @FT\_Open\_Face\ only\ tries\ to\ open}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02283\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ file\ with\ the\ driver\ whose\ handler\ is\ in\ `driver`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02284\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02285\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ the\ @FT\_OPEN\_PARAMS\ bit\ is\ set,\ the\ parameters\ given\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02286\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `num\_params`\ and\ `params`\ is\ used.\ \ They\ are\ ignored\ otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02287\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02288\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Ideally,\ both\ the\ `pathname`\ and\ `params`\ fields\ should\ be\ tagged\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02289\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 'const';\ this\ is\ missing\ for\ API\ backward\ compatibility.\ \ In\ other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02290\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ words,\ applications\ should\ treat\ them\ as\ read-\/only.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02291\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02292\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ \ }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_f_t___open___args__}{FT\_Open\_Args\_}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02409\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ face\_index\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02410\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ field\ holds\ two\ different\ values.\ \ Bits\ 0-\/15\ are\ the\ index\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02411\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ face\ in\ the\ font\ file\ (starting\ with\ value\string~0).\ \ Set\ it\ to\string~0\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02412\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ there\ is\ only\ one\ face\ in\ the\ font\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02413\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02414\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.6.1]\ Bits\ 16-\/30\ are\ relevant\ to\ GX\ and\ OpenType\ variation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02415\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ fonts\ only,\ specifying\ the\ named\ instance\ index\ for\ the\ current\ face}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02416\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ index\ (starting\ with\ value\string~1;\ value\string~0\ makes\ FreeType\ ignore\ named}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02417\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ instances).\ \ For\ non-\/variation\ fonts,\ bits\ 16-\/30\ are\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02418\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Assuming\ that\ you\ want\ to\ access\ the\ third\ named\ instance\ in\ face\string~4,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02419\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `face\_index`\ should\ be\ set\ to\ 0x00030004.\ \ If\ you\ want\ to\ access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02420\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ face\string~4\ without\ variation\ handling,\ simply\ set\ `face\_index`\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02421\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ value\string~4.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02422\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02423\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `FT\_Open\_Face`\ and\ its\ siblings\ can\ be\ used\ to\ quickly\ check\ whether}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02424\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ font\ format\ of\ a\ given\ font\ resource\ is\ supported\ by\ FreeType.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02425\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ In\ general,\ if\ the\ `face\_index`\ argument\ is\ negative,\ the\ function's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02426\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ return\ value\ is\string~0\ if\ the\ font\ format\ is\ recognized,\ or\ non-\/zero}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02427\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ otherwise.\ \ The\ function\ allocates\ a\ more\ or\ less\ empty\ face\ handle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02428\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ in\ `*aface`\ (if\ `aface`\ isn't\ `NULL`);\ the\ only\ two\ useful\ fields\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02429\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ this\ special\ case\ are\ `face-\/>num\_faces`\ and\ `face-\/>style\_flags`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02430\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ For\ any\ negative\ value\ of\ `face\_index`,\ `face-\/>num\_faces`\ gives\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02431\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ number\ of\ faces\ within\ the\ font\ file.\ \ For\ the\ negative\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02432\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ '-\/(N+1)'\ (with\ 'N'\ a\ non-\/negative\ 16-\/bit\ value),\ bits\ 16-\/30\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02433\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `face-\/>style\_flags`\ give\ the\ number\ of\ named\ instances\ in\ face\ 'N'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02434\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ if\ we\ have\ a\ variation\ font\ (or\ zero\ otherwise).\ \ After\ examination,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02435\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ returned\ @FT\_Face\ structure\ should\ be\ deallocated\ with\ a\ call\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02436\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Done\_Face.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02659\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Select\ a\ bitmap\ strike.\ \ To\ be\ more\ precise,\ this\ function\ sets\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ scaling\ factors\ of\ the\ active\ @FT\_Size\ object\ in\ a\ face\ so\ that}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02677\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ For\ bitmaps\ embedded\ in\ outline\ fonts\ it\ is\ common\ that\ only\ a\ subset}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02679\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ silently\ uses\ outlines\ if\ there\ is\ no\ bitmap\ for\ a\ given\ glyph\ index.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_Size\_Request\_Type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ An\ enumeration\ type\ that\ lists\ the\ supported\ size\ request\ types,\ i.e.,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ what\ input\ size\ (in\ font\ units)\ maps\ to\ the\ requested\ output\ size\ (in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02702\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ pixels,\ as\ computed\ from\ the\ arguments\ of\ @FT\_Size\_Request).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02703\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02704\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02705\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_NOMINAL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02706\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ nominal\ size.\ \ The\ `units\_per\_EM`\ field\ of\ @FT\_FaceRec\ is\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02707\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ to\ determine\ both\ scaling\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02708\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02709\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ is\ the\ standard\ scaling\ found\ in\ most\ applications.\ \ In}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02710\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ particular,\ use\ this\ size\ request\ type\ for\ TrueType\ fonts\ if\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02711\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ provide\ optical\ scaling\ or\ something\ similar.\ \ Note,\ however,\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02712\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `units\_per\_EM`\ is\ a\ rather\ abstract\ value\ which\ bears\ no\ relation\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02713\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ actual\ size\ of\ the\ glyphs\ in\ a\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02714\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02715\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_REAL\_DIM\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02716\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ real\ dimension.\ \ The\ sum\ of\ the\ `ascender`\ and\ (minus\ of)\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02717\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `descender`\ fields\ of\ @FT\_FaceRec\ is\ used\ to\ determine\ both\ scaling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02718\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02719\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02720\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_BBOX\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02721\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ font\ bounding\ box.\ \ The\ width\ and\ height\ of\ the\ `bbox`\ field\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02722\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_FaceRec\ are\ used\ to\ determine\ the\ horizontal\ and\ vertical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02723\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ scaling\ value,\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02724\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02725\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_CELL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02726\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ `max\_advance\_width`\ field\ of\ @FT\_FaceRec\ is\ used\ to\ determine}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02727\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ horizontal\ scaling\ value;\ the\ vertical\ scaling\ value\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02728\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ determined\ the\ same\ way\ as\ @FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_REAL\_DIM\ does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02729\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Finally,\ both\ scaling\ values\ are\ set\ to\ the\ smaller\ one.\ \ This\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02730\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ is\ useful\ if\ you\ want\ to\ specify\ the\ font\ size\ for,\ say,\ a\ window\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02731\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ a\ given\ dimension\ and\ 80x24\ cells.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02732\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02733\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_SCALES\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02734\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Specify\ the\ scaling\ values\ directly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02735\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02736\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02737\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ above\ descriptions\ only\ apply\ to\ scalable\ formats.\ \ For\ bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02738\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ formats,\ the\ behaviour\ is\ up\ to\ the\ driver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02739\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02740\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ See\ the\ note\ section\ of\ @FT\_Size\_Metrics\ if\ you\ wonder\ how\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02741\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ requesting\ relates\ to\ scaling\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02742\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02743\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \ FT\_Size\_Request\_Type\_}

\DoxyCodeLine{02775\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02776\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ horiResolution\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02777\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ horizontal\ resolution\ (dpi,\ i.e.,\ pixels\ per\ inch).\ \ If\ set\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02778\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ zero,\ `width`\ is\ treated\ as\ a\ 26.6\ fractional\ **pixel**\ value,\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02779\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ gets\ internally\ rounded\ to\ an\ integer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02780\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02781\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ vertResolution\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02782\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ vertical\ resolution\ (dpi,\ i.e.,\ pixels\ per\ inch).\ \ If\ set\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02783\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ zero,\ `height`\ is\ treated\ as\ a\ 26.6\ fractional\ **pixel**\ value,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02784\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ which\ gets\ internally\ rounded\ to\ an\ integer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02785\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02786\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02787\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ `width`\ is\ zero,\ the\ horizontal\ scaling\ value\ is\ set\ equal\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02788\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ vertical\ scaling\ value,\ and\ vice\ versa.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02789\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02790\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ `type`\ is\ `FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_SCALES`,\ `width`\ and\ `height`\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02791\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ interpreted\ directly\ as\ 16.16\ fractional\ scaling\ values,\ without\ any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02792\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ further\ modification,\ and\ both\ `horiResolution`\ and\ `vertResolution`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02793\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ are\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02794\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02839\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ bitmap\ strike.\ \ Use\ @FT\_Select\_Size\ instead\ in\ that\ case.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02844\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ this\ size.\ \ For\ more\ information\ refer\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02845\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 'https://www.freetype.org/freetype2/docs/glyphs/glyphs-\/2.html'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02846\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02847\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Contrary\ to\ @FT\_Set\_Char\_Size,\ this\ function\ doesn't\ have\ special\ code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02848\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ to\ normalize\ zero-\/valued\ widths,\ heights,\ or\ resolutions,\ which\ are}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02850\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
