\DoxyCodeLine{02896\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02897\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ character\ width\ or\ height\ smaller\ than\ 1pt\ is\ set\ to\ 1pt;\ if\ both}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02898\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ resolution\ values\ are\ zero,\ they\ are\ set\ to\ 72dpi.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ list\ of\ bit\ field\ constants\ for\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph\ to\ indicate\ what\ kind}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ of\ operations\ to\ perform\ during\ glyph\ loading.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_DEFAULT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Corresponding\ to\string~0,\ this\ value\ is\ used\ as\ the\ default\ glyph\ load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ operation.\ \ In\ this\ case,\ the\ following\ happens:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 1.\ FreeType\ looks\ for\ a\ bitmap\ for\ the\ glyph\ corresponding\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ face's\ current\ size.\ \ If\ one\ is\ found,\ the\ function\ returns.\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmap\ data\ can\ be\ accessed\ from\ the\ glyph\ slot\ (see\ note\ below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 2.\ If\ no\ embedded\ bitmap\ is\ searched\ for\ or\ found,\ FreeType\ looks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ for\ a\ scalable\ outline.\ \ If\ one\ is\ found,\ it\ is\ loaded\ from\ the\ font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ file,\ scaled\ to\ device\ pixels,\ then\ 'hinted'\ to\ the\ pixel\ grid\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ order\ to\ optimize\ it.\ \ The\ outline\ data\ can\ be\ accessed\ from\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyph\ slot\ (see\ note\ below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ by\ default\ the\ glyph\ loader\ doesn't\ render\ outlines\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmaps.\ \ The\ following\ flags\ are\ used\ to\ modify\ this\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ behaviour\ to\ more\ specific\ and\ useful\ cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Don't\ scale\ the\ loaded\ outline\ glyph\ but\ keep\ it\ in\ font\ units.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ also\ assumed\ if\ @FT\_Size\ owned\ by\ the\ face\ was\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ properly\ initialized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ implies\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING\ and\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ unsets\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ If\ the\ font\ is\ 'tricky'\ (see\ @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_TRICKY\ for\ more),\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE`\ usually\ yields\ meaningless\ outlines\ because\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ subglyphs\ must\ be\ scaled\ and\ positioned\ with\ hinting\ instructions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ can\ be\ solved\ by\ loading\ the\ font\ without\ `FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ and\ setting\ the\ character\ size\ to\ `font-\/>units\_per\_EM`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Disable\ hinting.\ \ This\ generally\ generates\ 'blurrier'\ bitmap\ glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ when\ the\ glyph\ are\ rendered\ in\ any\ of\ the\ anti-\/aliased\ modes.\ \ See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ also\ the\ note\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ implied\ by\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03086\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Call\ @FT\_Render\_Glyph\ after\ the\ glyph\ is\ loaded.\ \ By\ default,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyph\ is\ rendered\ in\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL\ mode.\ \ This\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ overridden\ by\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX\ or\ @FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ unset\ by\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03091\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Ignore\ bitmap\ strikes\ when\ loading.\ \ Bitmap-\/only\ fonts\ ignore\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03094\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ always\ sets\ this\ flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_SBITS\_ONLY\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.12]\ This\ is\ the\ opposite\ of\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP,\ more\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03100\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ less:\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph\ returns\ `FT\_Err\_Invalid\_Argument`\ if\ the\ face}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ contains\ a\ bitmap\ strike\ for\ the\ given\ size\ (or\ the\ strike\ selected}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ by\ @FT\_Select\_Size)\ but\ there\ is\ no\ glyph\ in\ the\ strike.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03104\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ this\ load\ flag\ was\ part\ of\ FreeType\ since\ version\ 2.0.6}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ but\ previously\ tagged\ as\ internal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03106\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_VERTICAL\_LAYOUT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Load\ the\ glyph\ for\ vertical\ text\ layout.\ \ In\ particular,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `advance`\ value\ in\ the\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ structure\ is\ set\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `vertAdvance`\ value\ of\ the\ `metrics`\ field.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03111\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ In\ case\ @FT\_HAS\_VERTICAL\ doesn't\ return\ true,\ you\ shouldn't\ use\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ flag\ currently.\ \ Reason\ is\ that\ in\ this\ case\ vertical\ metrics\ get}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ synthesized,\ and\ those\ values\ are\ not\ always\ consistent\ across}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03115\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ various\ font\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Prefer\ the\ auto-\/hinter\ over\ the\ font's\ native\ hinter.\ \ See\ also\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ note\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_PEDANTIC\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03122\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Make\ the\ font\ driver\ perform\ pedantic\ verifications\ during\ glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03123\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ loading\ and\ hinting.\ \ This\ is\ mostly\ used\ to\ detect\ broken\ glyphs\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ fonts.\ \ By\ default,\ FreeType\ tries\ to\ handle\ broken\ fonts\ also.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03125\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ In\ particular,\ errors\ from\ the\ TrueType\ bytecode\ engine\ are\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ passed\ to\ the\ application\ if\ this\ flag\ is\ not\ set;\ this\ might\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ in\ partially\ hinted\ or\ distorted\ glyphs\ in\ case\ a\ glyph's\ bytecode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ is\ buggy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03130\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_RECURSE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Don't\ load\ composite\ glyphs\ recursively.\ \ Instead,\ the\ font\ driver}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ fills\ the\ `num\_subglyph`\ and\ `subglyphs`\ values\ of\ the\ glyph\ slot;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ it\ also\ sets\ `glyph-\/>format`\ to\ @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_COMPOSITE.\ \ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ description\ of\ subglyphs\ can\ then\ be\ accessed\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Get\_SubGlyph\_Info.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Don't\ use\ this\ flag\ for\ retrieving\ metrics\ information\ since\ some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\ drivers\ only\ return\ rudimentary\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03141\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ implies\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ and\ @FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Ignore\ the\ transform\ matrix\ set\ by\ @FT\_Set\_Transform.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ used\ with\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ to\ indicate\ that\ you\ want\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ render\ an\ outline\ glyph\ to\ a\ 1-\/bit\ monochrome\ bitmap\ glyph,\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 8\string~pixels\ packed\ into\ each\ byte\ of\ the\ bitmap\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03150\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03151\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ this\ has\ no\ effect\ on\ the\ hinting\ algorithm\ used.\ \ You}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03152\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ should\ rather\ use\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO\ so\ that\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03153\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ monochrome-\/optimized\ hinting\ algorithm\ is\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03157\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ in\ font\ units.\ \ See\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ for\ details.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_COLOR\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03163\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Load\ colored\ glyphs.\ \ FreeType\ searches\ in\ the\ following\ order;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03164\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ there\ are\ slight\ differences\ depending\ on\ the\ font\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03165\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03166\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.5]\ Load\ embedded\ color\ bitmap\ images\ (provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03167\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP\ is\ not\ set).\ \ The\ resulting\ color\ bitmaps,\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03168\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ available,\ have\ the\ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_BGRA\ format,\ with\ pre-\/multiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03169\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ color\ channels.\ \ If\ the\ flag\ is\ not\ set\ and\ color\ bitmaps\ are\ found,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03170\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ they\ are\ converted\ to\ 256-\/level\ gray\ bitmaps,\ using\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03171\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_GRAY\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03172\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03173\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.12]\ If\ the\ glyph\ index\ maps\ to\ an\ entry\ in\ the\ face's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03174\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'SVG\string~'\ table,\ load\ the\ associated\ SVG\ document\ from\ this\ table\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03175\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ set\ the\ `format`\ field\ of\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ to\ @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_SVG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03176\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ FreeType\ itself\ can't\ render\ SVG\ documents;\ however,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03177\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ library\ provides\ hooks\ to\ seamlessly\ integrate\ an\ external\ renderer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03178\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ See\ sections\ @ot\_svg\_driver\ and\ @svg\_fonts\ for\ more.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03179\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03180\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.10,\ experimental]\ If\ the\ glyph\ index\ maps\ to\ an\ entry\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ face's\ 'COLR'\ table\ with\ a\ 'CPAL'\ palette\ table\ (as\ defined\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03182\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ OpenType\ specification),\ make\ @FT\_Render\_Glyph\ provide\ a\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ blending\ of\ the\ color\ glyph\ layers\ associated\ with\ the\ glyph\ index,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03184\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ using\ the\ same\ bitmap\ format\ as\ embedded\ color\ bitmap\ images.\ \ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ is\ mainly\ for\ convenience\ and\ works\ only\ for\ glyphs\ in\ 'COLR'\ v0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ tables\ (or\ glyphs\ in\ 'COLR'\ v1\ tables\ that\ exclusively\ use\ v0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ features).\ \ For\ full\ control\ of\ color\ layers\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Get\_Color\_Glyph\_Layer\ and\ FreeType's\ color\ functions\ like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Palette\_Select\ instead\ of\ setting\ @FT\_LOAD\_COLOR\ for\ rendering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ so\ that\ the\ client\ application\ can\ handle\ blending\ by\ itself.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_COMPUTE\_METRICS\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ [Since\ 2.6.1]\ Compute\ glyph\ metrics\ from\ the\ glyph\ data,\ without\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ use\ of\ bundled\ metrics\ tables\ (for\ example,\ the\ 'hdmx'\ table\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ TrueType\ fonts).\ \ This\ flag\ is\ mainly\ used\ by\ font\ validating\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\ editing\ applications,\ which\ need\ to\ ignore,\ verify,\ or\ edit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ those\ tables.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Currently,\ this\ flag\ is\ only\ implemented\ for\ TrueType\ fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03272\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ hinter.\ \ You\ should\ OR\ one\ of\ these\ values\ to\ your\ `load\_flags`\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03273\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ calling\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03274\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03275\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Note\ that\ a\ font's\ native\ hinters\ may\ ignore\ the\ hinting\ algorithm\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03276\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ have\ specified\ (e.g.,\ the\ TrueType\ bytecode\ interpreter).\ \ You\ can\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03277\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT\ to\ ensure\ that\ the\ auto-\/hinter\ is\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03278\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03279\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03280\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03281\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ default\ hinting\ algorithm,\ optimized\ for\ standard\ gray-\/level}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03282\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ rendering.\ \ For\ monochrome\ output,\ use\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03283\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03284\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03285\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ lighter\ hinting\ algorithm\ for\ gray-\/level\ modes.\ \ Many\ generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03286\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyphs\ are\ fuzzier\ but\ better\ resemble\ their\ original\ shape.\ \ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03287\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ is\ achieved\ by\ snapping\ glyphs\ to\ the\ pixel\ grid\ only\ vertically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03288\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (Y-\/axis),\ as\ is\ done\ by\ FreeType's\ new\ CFF\ engine\ or\ Microsoft's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03289\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ ClearType\ font\ renderer.\ \ This\ preserves\ inter-\/glyph\ spacing\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03290\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ horizontal\ text.\ \ The\ snapping\ is\ done\ either\ by\ the\ native\ font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03291\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ driver,\ if\ the\ driver\ itself\ and\ the\ font\ support\ it,\ or\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03292\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ auto-\/hinter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03293\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03294\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Advance\ widths\ are\ rounded\ to\ integer\ values;\ however,\ using\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03295\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ `lsb\_delta`\ and\ `rsb\_delta`\ fields\ of\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec,\ it\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03296\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ possible\ to\ get\ fractional\ advance\ widths\ for\ subpixel\ positioning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03297\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (which\ is\ recommended\ to\ use).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03298\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03299\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ If\ configuration\ option\ `AF\_CONFIG\_OPTION\_TT\_SIZE\_METRICS`\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03300\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ active,\ TrueType-\/like\ metrics\ are\ used\ to\ make\ this\ mode\ behave}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03301\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ similarly\ as\ in\ unpatched\ FreeType\ versions\ between\ 2.4.6\ and\ 2.7.1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03302\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (inclusive).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03303\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03304\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03305\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Strong\ hinting\ algorithm\ that\ should\ only\ be\ used\ for\ monochrome}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03306\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ output.\ \ The\ result\ is\ probably\ unpleasant\ if\ the\ glyph\ is\ rendered}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03307\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ in\ non-\/monochrome\ modes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03308\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03309\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ for\ outline\ fonts\ only\ the\ TrueType\ font\ driver\ has\ proper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03310\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ monochrome\ hinting\ support,\ provided\ the\ TTFs\ contain\ hints\ for\ B/W}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03311\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ rendering\ (which\ most\ fonts\ no\ longer\ provide).\ \ If\ these\ conditions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03312\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ are\ not\ met\ it\ is\ very\ likely\ that\ you\ get\ ugly\ results\ at\ smaller}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03313\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ sizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03314\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03315\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LCD\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03316\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ variant\ of\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT\ optimized\ for\ horizontally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03317\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ decimated\ LCD\ displays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03318\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03319\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LCD\_V\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03320\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ variant\ of\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL\ optimized\ for\ vertically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03321\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ decimated\ LCD\ displays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03322\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03323\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03324\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ You\ should\ use\ only\ \_one\_\ of\ the\ `FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX`\ values\ in\ your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03325\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ `load\_flags`.\ \ They\ can't\ be\ ORed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03326\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03327\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ is\ also\ set,\ the\ glyph\ is\ rendered\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03328\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ corresponding\ mode\ (i.e.,\ the\ mode\ that\ matches\ the\ used\ algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03329\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ best).\ \ An\ exception\ is\ `FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO`\ since\ it\ implies}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03330\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03331\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03332\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ You\ can\ use\ a\ hinting\ algorithm\ that\ doesn't\ correspond\ to\ the\ same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03333\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ rendering\ mode.\ \ As\ an\ example,\ it\ is\ possible\ to\ use\ the\ 'light'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03334\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ hinting\ algorithm\ and\ have\ the\ results\ rendered\ in\ horizontal\ LCD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03335\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ pixel\ mode,\ with\ code\ like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03336\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03337\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03338\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_Load\_Glyph(\ face,\ glyph\_index,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03339\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ load\_flags\ |\ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03340\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03341\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_Render\_Glyph(\ face-\/>glyph,\ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03342\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03343\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03344\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ In\ general,\ you\ should\ stick\ with\ one\ rendering\ mode.\ \ For\ example,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03345\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ switching\ between\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL\ and\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03346\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ enforces\ a\ lot\ of\ recomputation\ for\ TrueType\ fonts,\ which\ is\ slow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03347\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Another\ reason\ is\ caching:\ Selecting\ a\ different\ mode\ usually\ causes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03348\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ changes\ in\ both\ the\ outlines\ and\ the\ rasterized\ bitmaps;\ it\ is\ thus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03349\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ necessary\ to\ empty\ the\ cache\ after\ a\ mode\ switch\ to\ avoid\ false\ hits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03350\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03351\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03352\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_(\ x\ )\ \ \ (\ FT\_STATIC\_CAST(\ FT\_Int32,\ (x)\ \&\ 15\ )\ <<\ 16\ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03353\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03450\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03451\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03452\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03453\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_Render\_Mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03454\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03455\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03456\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Render\ modes\ supported\ by\ FreeType\string~2.\ \ Each\ mode\ corresponds\ to\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03457\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ specific\ type\ of\ scanline\ conversion\ performed\ on\ the\ outline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03458\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ For\ bitmap\ fonts\ and\ embedded\ bitmaps\ the\ `bitmap-\/>pixel\_mode`\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ in\ the\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ structure\ gives\ the\ format\ of\ the\ returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ bitmap.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ All\ modes\ except\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO\ use\ 256\ levels\ of\ opacity,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ indicating\ pixel\ coverage.\ \ Use\ linear\ alpha\ blending\ and\ gamma}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ correction\ to\ correctly\ render\ non-\/monochrome\ glyph\ bitmaps\ onto\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03466\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ surface;\ see\ @FT\_Render\_Glyph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_SDF\ is\ a\ special\ render\ mode\ that\ uses\ up\ to\ 256}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03469\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ distance\ values,\ indicating\ the\ signed\ distance\ from\ the\ grid\ position}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03470\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ to\ the\ nearest\ outline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03471\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03474\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Default\ render\ mode;\ it\ corresponds\ to\ 8-\/bit\ anti-\/aliased\ bitmaps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03475\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03476\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LIGHT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03477\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ is\ equivalent\ to\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL.\ \ It\ is\ only\ defined\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03478\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ a\ separate\ value\ because\ render\ modes\ are\ also\ used\ indirectly\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03479\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ define\ hinting\ algorithm\ selectors.\ \ See\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03480\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03481\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03482\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03483\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ mode\ corresponds\ to\ 1-\/bit\ bitmaps\ (with\ 2\string~levels\ of\ opacity).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03484\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03485\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03486\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ mode\ corresponds\ to\ horizontal\ RGB\ and\ BGR\ subpixel\ displays}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03487\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ like\ LCD\ screens.\ \ It\ produces\ 8-\/bit\ bitmaps\ that\ are\ 3\string~times\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03488\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ width\ of\ the\ original\ glyph\ outline\ in\ pixels,\ and\ which\ use\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03489\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_LCD\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03490\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03491\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD\_V\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03492\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ mode\ corresponds\ to\ vertical\ RGB\ and\ BGR\ subpixel\ displays}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03493\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (like\ PDA\ screens,\ rotated\ LCD\ displays,\ etc.).\ \ It\ produces\ 8-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03494\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmaps\ that\ are\ 3\string~times\ the\ height\ of\ the\ original\ glyph\ outline\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03495\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ pixels\ and\ use\ the\ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_LCD\_V\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03496\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03497\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_SDF\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03498\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ mode\ corresponds\ to\ 8-\/bit,\ single-\/channel\ signed\ distance\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03499\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ (SDF)\ bitmaps.\ \ Each\ pixel\ in\ the\ SDF\ grid\ is\ the\ value\ from\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03500\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ pixel's\ position\ to\ the\ nearest\ glyph's\ outline.\ \ The\ distances\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03501\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ calculated\ from\ the\ center\ of\ the\ pixel\ and\ are\ positive\ if\ they\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03502\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ filled\ by\ the\ outline\ (i.e.,\ inside\ the\ outline)\ and\ negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03503\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ otherwise.\ \ Check\ the\ note\ below\ on\ how\ to\ convert\ the\ output\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03504\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ to\ usable\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03505\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03506\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03507\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ selected\ render\ mode\ only\ affects\ vector\ glyphs\ of\ a\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03508\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Embedded\ bitmaps\ often\ have\ a\ different\ pixel\ mode\ like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03509\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_MONO.\ \ You\ can\ use\ @FT\_Bitmap\_Convert\ to\ transform\ them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03510\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ into\ 8-\/bit\ pixmaps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03511\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03512\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ For\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_SDF\ the\ output\ bitmap\ buffer\ contains\ normalized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03513\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ distances\ that\ are\ packed\ into\ unsigned\ 8-\/bit\ values.\ \ To\ get\ pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03514\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ values\ in\ floating\ point\ representation\ use\ the\ following\ pseudo-\/C}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03515\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ code\ for\ the\ conversion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03516\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03517\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03518\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ //\ Load\ glyph\ and\ render\ using\ FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_SDF,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03519\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ //\ then\ use\ the\ output\ buffer\ as\ follows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03520\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03521\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03522\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_Byte\ \ buffer\ =\ glyph-\/>bitmap-\/>buffer;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03523\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03524\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03525\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ for\ pixel\ in\ buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03526\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03527\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ //\ `sd`\ is\ the\ signed\ distance\ and\ `spread`\ is\ the\ current\ spread;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03528\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ //\ the\ default\ spread\ is\ 2\ and\ can\ be\ changed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03529\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03530\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ float\ \ sd\ =\ (float)pixel\ -\/\ 128.0f;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03531\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03532\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03533\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ //\ Convert\ to\ pixel\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03534\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ sd\ =\ (\ sd\ /\ 128.0f\ )\ *\ spread;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03535\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03536\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ //\ Store\ `sd`\ in\ a\ buffer\ or\ use\ as\ required.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03537\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03538\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03539\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03540\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03541\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ has\ two\ rasterizers\ for\ generating\ SDF,\ namely:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03542\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03543\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 1.\ `sdf`\ for\ generating\ SDF\ directly\ from\ glyph's\ outline,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03544\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03545\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 2.\ `bsdf`\ for\ generating\ SDF\ from\ rasterized\ bitmaps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03546\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Depending\ on\ the\ glyph\ type\ (i.e.,\ outline\ or\ bitmap),\ one\ of\ the\ two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ rasterizers\ is\ chosen\ at\ runtime\ and\ used\ for\ generating\ SDFs.\ \ To}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ force\ the\ use\ of\ `bsdf`\ you\ should\ render\ the\ glyph\ with\ any\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType's\ other\ rendering\ modes\ (e.g.,\ `FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL`)\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ then\ re-\/render\ with\ `FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_SDF`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03552\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ There\ are\ some\ issues\ with\ stability\ and\ possible\ failures\ of\ the\ SDF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03554\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ renderers\ (specifically\ `sdf`).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03555\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03556\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 1.\ The\ `sdf`\ rasterizer\ is\ sensitive\ to\ really\ small\ features\ (e.g.,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03557\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sharp\ turns\ that\ are\ less\ than\ 1\string~pixel)\ and\ imperfections\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ glyph's\ outline,\ causing\ artifacts\ in\ the\ final\ output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03560\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 2.\ The\ `sdf`\ rasterizer\ has\ limited\ support\ for\ handling\ intersecting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03561\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ contours\ and\ *cannot*\ handle\ self-\/intersecting\ contours\ whatsoever.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03562\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ Self-\/intersection\ happens\ when\ a\ single\ connected\ contour\ intersect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03563\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ itself\ at\ some\ point;\ having\ these\ in\ your\ font\ definitely\ pose\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03564\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ problem\ to\ the\ rasterizer\ and\ cause\ artifacts,\ too.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03565\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03566\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 3.\ Generating\ SDF\ for\ really\ small\ glyphs\ may\ result\ in\ undesirable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03567\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ output;\ the\ pixel\ grid\ (which\ stores\ distance\ information)\ becomes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03568\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ too\ coarse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03569\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03570\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 4.\ Since\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ normalized,\ precision\ at\ smaller\ spreads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03571\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ is\ greater\ than\ precision\ at\ larger\ spread\ values\ because\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03572\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ output\ range\ of\ [0..255]\ gets\ mapped\ to\ a\ smaller\ SDF\ range.\ \ A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03573\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ spread\ of\string~2\ should\ be\ sufficient\ in\ most\ cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03574\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03575\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Points\ (1)\ and\ (2)\ can\ be\ avoided\ by\ using\ the\ `bsdf`\ rasterizer,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03576\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ which\ is\ more\ stable\ than\ the\ `sdf`\ rasterizer\ in\ general.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03577\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03578\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03579\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \ FT\_Render\_Mode\_}

\DoxyCodeLine{03600\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03601\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03602\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_Render\_Glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03603\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03604\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03605\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Convert\ a\ given\ glyph\ image\ to\ a\ bitmap.\ \ It\ does\ so\ by\ inspecting\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03606\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ glyph\ image\ format,\ finding\ the\ relevant\ renderer,\ and\ invoking\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03607\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03608\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @inout:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03609\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ slot\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03610\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ handle\ to\ the\ glyph\ slot\ containing\ the\ image\ to\ convert.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03611\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03612\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @input:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03613\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ render\_mode\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03614\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ render\ mode\ used\ to\ render\ the\ glyph\ image\ into\ a\ bitmap.\ \ See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03615\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_Render\_Mode\ for\ a\ list\ of\ possible\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03616\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03617\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ If\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL\ is\ used,\ a\ previous\ call\ of\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03618\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ with\ flag\ @FT\_LOAD\_COLOR\ makes\ `FT\_Render\_Glyph`\ provide\ a\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03619\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ blending\ of\ colored\ glyph\ layers\ associated\ with\ the\ current\ glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03620\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ slot\ (provided\ the\ font\ contains\ such\ layers)\ instead\ of\ rendering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03621\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ the\ glyph\ slot's\ outline.\ \ This\ is\ an\ experimental\ feature;\ see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03622\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_COLOR\ for\ more\ information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03623\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03624\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @return:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03625\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FreeType\ error\ code.\ \ 0\string~means\ success.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03626\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03627\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03628\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ When\ FreeType\ outputs\ a\ bitmap\ of\ a\ glyph,\ it\ really\ outputs\ an\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03629\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ coverage\ map.\ \ If\ a\ pixel\ is\ completely\ covered\ by\ a\ filled-\/in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03630\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ outline,\ the\ bitmap\ contains\ 0xFF\ at\ that\ pixel,\ meaning\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03631\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 0xFF/0xFF\ fraction\ of\ that\ pixel\ is\ covered,\ meaning\ the\ pixel\ is\ 100\%}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03632\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ black\ (or\ 0\%\ bright).\ \ If\ a\ pixel\ is\ only\ 50\%\ covered\ (value\ 0x80),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03633\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ pixel\ is\ made\ 50\%\ black\ (50\%\ bright\ or\ a\ middle\ shade\ of\ grey).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03634\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 0\%\ covered\ means\ 0\%\ black\ (100\%\ bright\ or\ white).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03635\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03636\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ On\ high-\/DPI\ screens\ like\ on\ smartphones\ and\ tablets,\ the\ pixels\ are\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03637\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ small\ that\ their\ chance\ of\ being\ completely\ covered\ and\ therefore}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03638\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ completely\ black\ are\ fairly\ good.\ \ On\ the\ low-\/DPI\ screens,\ however,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03639\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ situation\ is\ different.\ \ The\ pixels\ are\ too\ large\ for\ most\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03640\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ details\ of\ a\ glyph\ and\ shades\ of\ gray\ are\ the\ norm\ rather\ than\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03641\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ exception.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03642\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03643\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ This\ is\ relevant\ because\ all\ our\ screens\ have\ a\ second\ problem:\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03644\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ are\ not\ linear.\ \ 1\string~+\string~1\ is\ not\string~2.\ \ Twice\ the\ value\ does\ not\ result\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03645\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ twice\ the\ brightness.\ \ When\ a\ pixel\ is\ only\ 50\%\ covered,\ the\ coverage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03646\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ map\ says\ 50\%\ black,\ and\ this\ translates\ to\ a\ pixel\ value\ of\ 128\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03647\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ you\ use\ 8\string~bits\ per\ channel\ (0-\/255).\ \ However,\ this\ does\ not\ translate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03648\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ to\ 50\%\ brightness\ for\ that\ pixel\ on\ our\ sRGB\ and\ gamma\string~2.2\ screens.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03649\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Due\ to\ their\ non-\/linearity,\ they\ dwell\ longer\ in\ the\ darks\ and\ only\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03650\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ pixel\ value\ of\ about\ 186\ results\ in\ 50\%\ brightness\ -\/-\/\ 128\ ends\ up\ too}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03651\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ dark\ on\ both\ bright\ and\ dark\ backgrounds.\ \ The\ net\ result\ is\ that\ dark}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03652\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ text\ looks\ burnt-\/out,\ pixely\ and\ blotchy\ on\ bright\ background,\ bright}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ text\ too\ frail\ on\ dark\ backgrounds,\ and\ colored\ text\ on\ colored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03654\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ background\ (for\ example,\ red\ on\ green)\ seems\ to\ have\ dark\ halos\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 'dirt'\ around\ it.\ \ The\ situation\ is\ especially\ ugly\ for\ diagonal\ stems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03656\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ like\ in\ 'w'\ glyph\ shapes\ where\ the\ quality\ of\ FreeType's\ anti-\/aliasing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03657\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ depends\ on\ the\ correct\ display\ of\ grays.\ \ On\ high-\/DPI\ screens\ where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03658\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ smaller,\ fully\ black\ pixels\ reign\ supreme,\ this\ doesn't\ matter,\ but\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03659\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ our\ low-\/DPI\ screens\ with\ all\ the\ gray\ shades,\ it\ does.\ \ 0\%\ and\ 100\%}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ brightness\ are\ the\ same\ things\ in\ linear\ and\ non-\/linear\ space,\ just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03661\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ all\ the\ shades\ in-\/between\ aren't.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03662\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03663\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ blending\ function\ for\ placing\ text\ over\ a\ background\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03664\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03665\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03666\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ dst\ =\ alpha\ *\ src\ +\ (1\ -\/\ alpha)\ *\ dst\ \ \ \ ,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03667\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03668\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03669\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ which\ is\ known\ as\ the\ OVER\ operator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03670\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03671\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ To\ correctly\ composite\ an\ anti-\/aliased\ pixel\ of\ a\ glyph\ onto\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03672\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ surface,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03673\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03674\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 1.\ take\ the\ foreground\ and\ background\ colors\ (e.g.,\ in\ sRGB\ space)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03675\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ and\ apply\ gamma\ to\ get\ them\ in\ a\ linear\ space,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03676\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03677\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 2.\ use\ OVER\ to\ blend\ the\ two\ linear\ colors\ using\ the\ glyph\ pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03678\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ as\ the\ alpha\ value\ (remember,\ the\ glyph\ bitmap\ is\ an\ alpha\ coverage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03679\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ bitmap),\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03680\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03681\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 3.\ apply\ inverse\ gamma\ to\ the\ blended\ pixel\ and\ write\ it\ back\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03682\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ the\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03683\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03684\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Internal\ testing\ at\ Adobe\ found\ that\ a\ target\ inverse\ gamma\ of\string~1.8\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03685\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ step\string~3\ gives\ good\ results\ across\ a\ wide\ range\ of\ displays\ with\ an\ sRGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03686\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ gamma\ curve\ or\ a\ similar\ one.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03687\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03688\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ This\ process\ can\ cost\ performance.\ \ There\ is\ an\ approximation\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03689\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ does\ not\ need\ to\ know\ about\ the\ background\ color;\ see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03690\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ https://bel.fi/alankila/lcd/\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03691\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ https://bel.fi/alankila/lcd/alpcor.html\ for\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03692\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03693\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ **ATTENTION**:\ Linear\ blending\ is\ even\ more\ important\ when\ dealing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03694\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ with\ subpixel-\/rendered\ glyphs\ to\ prevent\ color-\/fringing!\ \ A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ subpixel-\/rendered\ glyph\ must\ first\ be\ filtered\ with\ a\ filter\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ gives\ equal\ weight\ to\ the\ three\ color\ primaries\ and\ does\ not\ exceed\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ sum\ of\ 0x100,\ see\ section\ @lcd\_rendering.\ \ Then\ the\ only\ difference\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ gray\ linear\ blending\ is\ that\ subpixel-\/rendered\ linear\ blending\ is\ done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 3\string~times\ per\ pixel:\ red\ foreground\ subpixel\ to\ red\ background\ subpixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ and\ so\ on\ for\ green\ and\ blue.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03702\ \ \ FT\_EXPORT(\ FT\_Error\ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{03703\ \ \ FT\_Render\_Glyph(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_f_t___glyph_slot_rec__}{FT\_GlyphSlot}}\ \ \ \ slot,}

\DoxyCodeLine{04031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ you\ use\ FreeType\ to\ manipulate\ the\ contents\ of\ font\ files\ directly,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ be\ aware\ that\ the\ glyph\ index\ returned\ by\ this\ function\ doesn't\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ correspond\ to\ the\ internal\ indices\ used\ within\ the\ file.\ \ This\ is\ done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ to\ ensure\ that\ value\string~0\ always\ corresponds\ to\ the\ 'missing\ glyph'.\ \ If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ first\ glyph\ is\ not\ named\ '.notdef',\ then\ for\ Type\string~1\ and\ Type\string~42}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ fonts,\ '.notdef'\ will\ be\ moved\ into\ the\ glyph\ ID\string~0\ position,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ whatever\ was\ there\ will\ be\ moved\ to\ the\ position\ '.notdef'\ had.\ \ For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Type\string~1\ fonts,\ if\ there\ is\ no\ '.notdef'\ glyph\ at\ all,\ then\ one\ will\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ created\ at\ index\string~0\ and\ whatever\ was\ there\ will\ be\ moved\ to\ the\ last}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ index\ -\/-\/\ Type\string~42\ fonts\ are\ considered\ invalid\ under\ this\ condition.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ You\ should\ use\ this\ function\ together\ with\ @FT\_Get\_Next\_Char\ to\ parse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ all\ character\ codes\ available\ in\ a\ given\ charmap.\ \ The\ code\ should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ look\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_ULong\ \ charcode;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_UInt\ \ \ gindex;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ charcode\ =\ FT\_Get\_First\_Char(\ face,\ \&gindex\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ while\ (\ gindex\ !=\ 0\ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ...\ do\ something\ with\ (charcode,gindex)\ pair\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ charcode\ =\ FT\_Get\_Next\_Char(\ face,\ charcode,\ \&gindex\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04086\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Be\ aware\ that\ character\ codes\ can\ have\ values\ up\ to\ 0xFFFFFFFF;\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ might\ happen\ for\ non-\/Unicode\ or\ malformed\ cmaps.\ \ However,\ even\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ regular\ Unicode\ encoding,\ so-\/called\ 'last\ resort\ fonts'\ (using\ SFNT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04091\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ cmap\ format\ 13,\ see\ function\ @FT\_Get\_CMap\_Format)\ normally\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ entries\ for\ all\ Unicode\ characters\ up\ to\ 0x1FFFFF,\ which\ can\ cause\ *a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ lot*\ of\ iterations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04094\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Note\ that\ `*agindex`\ is\ set\ to\string~0\ if\ the\ charmap\ is\ empty.\ \ The\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ itself\ can\ be\string~0\ in\ two\ cases:\ if\ the\ charmap\ is\ empty\ or\ if\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ value\string~0\ is\ the\ first\ valid\ character\ code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04099\ \ \ FT\_EXPORT(\ FT\_ULong\ )}

\DoxyCodeLine{04361\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04362\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ list\ of\ bit\ flags\ used\ in\ the\ `fsType`\ field\ of\ the\ OS/2\ table\ in\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04363\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ TrueType\ or\ OpenType\ font\ and\ the\ `FSType`\ entry\ in\ a\ PostScript\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04364\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ These\ bit\ flags\ are\ returned\ by\ @FT\_Get\_FSType\_Flags;\ they\ inform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04365\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ client\ applications\ of\ embedding\ and\ subsetting\ restrictions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04366\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ associated\ with\ a\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04367\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04368\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04369\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ https://www.adobe.com/content/dam/Adobe/en/devnet/acrobat/pdfs/FontPolicies.pdf}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04370\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ for\ more\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04371\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04372\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04373\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FSTYPE\_INSTALLABLE\_EMBEDDING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04374\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Fonts\ with\ no\ fsType\ bit\ set\ may\ be\ embedded\ and\ permanently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04375\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ installed\ on\ the\ remote\ system\ by\ an\ application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04376\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04377\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FSTYPE\_RESTRICTED\_LICENSE\_EMBEDDING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04378\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Fonts\ that\ have\ only\ this\ bit\ set\ must\ not\ be\ modified,\ embedded\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04379\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ exchanged\ in\ any\ manner\ without\ first\ obtaining\ permission\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04380\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ font\ software\ copyright\ owner.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04381\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04382\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FSTYPE\_PREVIEW\_AND\_PRINT\_EMBEDDING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04383\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ font\ may\ be\ embedded\ and\ temporarily\ loaded\ on\ the\ remote}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04384\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ system.\ \ Documents\ containing\ Preview\ \&\ Print\ fonts\ must\ be\ opened}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04385\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 'read-\/only';\ no\ edits\ can\ be\ applied\ to\ the\ document.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04386\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04387\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FSTYPE\_EDITABLE\_EMBEDDING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04388\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ font\ may\ be\ embedded\ but\ must\ only\ be\ installed\ temporarily\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04389\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ other\ systems.\ \ In\ contrast\ to\ Preview\ \&\ Print\ fonts,\ documents}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04390\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ containing\ editable\ fonts\ may\ be\ opened\ for\ reading,\ editing\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04391\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ permitted,\ and\ changes\ may\ be\ saved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04392\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04393\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FSTYPE\_NO\_SUBSETTING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04394\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ The\ font\ may\ not\ be\ subsetted\ prior\ to\ embedding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04395\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04396\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_FSTYPE\_BITMAP\_EMBEDDING\_ONLY\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04397\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Only\ bitmaps\ contained\ in\ the\ font\ may\ be\ embedded;\ no\ outline\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04398\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ may\ be\ embedded.\ \ If\ there\ are\ no\ bitmaps\ available\ in\ the\ font,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04399\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ then\ the\ font\ is\ unembeddable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04400\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04401\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04402\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ flags\ are\ ORed\ together,\ thus\ more\ than\ a\ single\ value\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04403\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ returned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04404\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04405\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ While\ the\ `fsType`\ flags\ can\ indicate\ that\ a\ font\ may\ be\ embedded,\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04406\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ license\ with\ the\ font\ vendor\ may\ be\ separately\ required\ to\ use\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04407\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ font\ in\ this\ way.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04408\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04445\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04446\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04447\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @section:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04448\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ glyph\_variants}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04449\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04450\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @title:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04451\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Unicode\ Variation\ Sequences}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04452\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04453\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @abstract:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04454\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ FreeType\string~2\ interface\ to\ Unicode\ Variation\ Sequences\ (UVS),\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04455\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ the\ SFNT\ cmap\ format\string~14.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04456\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04457\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04458\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Many\ characters,\ especially\ for\ CJK\ scripts,\ have\ variant\ forms.\ \ They}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ are\ a\ sort\ of\ grey\ area\ somewhere\ between\ being\ totally\ irrelevant\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ semantically\ distinct;\ for\ this\ reason,\ the\ Unicode\ consortium\ decided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ to\ introduce\ Variation\ Sequences\ (VS),\ consisting\ of\ a\ Unicode\ base}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ character\ and\ a\ variation\ selector\ instead\ of\ further\ extending\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ already\ huge\ number\ of\ characters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Unicode\ maintains\ two\ different\ sets,\ namely\ 'Standardized\ Variation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04466\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Sequences'\ and\ registered\ 'Ideographic\ Variation\ Sequences'\ (IVS),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ collected\ in\ the\ 'Ideographic\ Variation\ Database'\ (IVD).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04469\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ https://unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/StandardizedVariants.txt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04470\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ https://unicode.org/reports/tr37/\ https://unicode.org/ivd/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04471\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ To\ date\ (January\ 2017),\ the\ character\ with\ the\ most\ ideographic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ variations\ is\ U+9089,\ having\ 32\ such\ IVS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04474\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04475\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Three\ Mongolian\ Variation\ Selectors\ have\ the\ values\ U+180B-\/U+180D;\ 256}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04476\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ generic\ Variation\ Selectors\ are\ encoded\ in\ the\ ranges\ U+FE00-\/U+FE0F}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04477\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ and\ U+E0100-\/U+E01EF.\ \ IVS\ currently\ use\ Variation\ Selectors\ from\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04478\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ range\ U+E0100-\/U+E01EF\ only.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04479\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04480\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ VS\ consists\ of\ the\ base\ character\ value\ followed\ by\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04481\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Variation\ Selector.\ \ For\ example,\ to\ get\ the\ first\ variation\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04482\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ U+9089,\ you\ have\ to\ write\ the\ character\ sequence\ `U+9089\ U+E0100`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04483\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04484\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ Adobe\ and\ MS\ decided\ to\ support\ both\ standardized\ and\ ideographic\ VS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04485\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ with\ a\ new\ cmap\ subtable\ (format\string~14).\ \ It\ is\ an\ odd\ subtable\ because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04486\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ it\ is\ not\ a\ mapping\ of\ input\ code\ points\ to\ glyphs,\ but\ contains\ lists}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04487\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ of\ all\ variations\ supported\ by\ the\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04488\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04489\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ variation\ may\ be\ either\ 'default'\ or\ 'non-\/default'\ for\ a\ given\ font.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04490\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ default\ variation\ is\ the\ one\ you\ will\ get\ for\ that\ code\ point\ if\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04491\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ look\ it\ up\ in\ the\ standard\ Unicode\ cmap.\ \ A\ non-\/default\ variation\ is\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04492\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ different\ glyph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04493\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04494\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04495\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04496\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04497\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04498\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04499\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @function:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04515\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04516\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @return:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04517\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ The\ glyph\ index.\ \ 0\string~means\ either\ 'undefined\ character\ code',\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04518\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 'undefined\ selector\ code',\ or\ 'no\ variation\ selector\ cmap\ subtable',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04519\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ or\ 'current\ CharMap\ is\ not\ Unicode'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04520\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04521\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04522\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ you\ use\ FreeType\ to\ manipulate\ the\ contents\ of\ font\ files\ directly,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04523\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ be\ aware\ that\ the\ glyph\ index\ returned\ by\ this\ function\ doesn't\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04524\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ correspond\ to\ the\ internal\ indices\ used\ within\ the\ file.\ \ This\ is\ done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04525\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ to\ ensure\ that\ value\string~0\ always\ corresponds\ to\ the\ 'missing\ glyph'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04526\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04527\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ This\ function\ is\ only\ meaningful\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04528\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ a)\ the\ font\ has\ a\ variation\ selector\ cmap\ sub\ table,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04529\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ b)\ the\ current\ charmap\ has\ a\ Unicode\ encoding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04530\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04531\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @since:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04532\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ 2.3.6}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04533\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04534\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04535\ \ \ FT\_EXPORT(\ FT\_UInt\ )}

\DoxyCodeLine{04773\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ argument\ of\ this\ function;\ this\ can\ make\ a\ great\ difference.}}
